<L.6.1>
<Z>Gridiron Stats <C> Gridiron Stats has just restarted for the new season, so if you want to get in early as the bidding for the<L.31.1>
rookies starts, now is the time. Gridiron Stats is a trading game running throughout the NFL Season. You coach a team of NFL<L.31.1>
Stars, every week throughout the season, trading, signing and poaching players. Startup, rules and first three turns for a fiver.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Online Orders <C> If you submit your orders online, the confirmation that they've been received by us is the page that comes up<L.31.1>
in response to you pushing the button. When you see that page, your orders are in. The version that's emailed to you is just for<L.31.1>
information - we email it to save you having to copy and paste or save it as a screenshot. If the email copy of your orders<L.31.1>
doesn't appear don't worry about it - emails get delayed or go missing quite often (far more than some people think).<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Email Results <C> Emailed results are normally sent out between 3pm and 6pm. If there's a delay in processing, it'll say so on<L.31.1>
www.pbmsports.com - please check there first. If you haven't received emailed results 24 hours after they're due, then email me<L.31.1>
and ask for them to be resent. Don't ask me before the 24 hours are due, but don't wait much longer either.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Email Game Reports <C> There's a downloads page on www.sidetracks.co.uk with the printing utility and a sample game report, so<L.31.1>
you can try the printing program without needing anything more from us. Email reports are available for ALL games. You can receive<L.31.1>
results by email AND post (because you like the quality of our printers) if you wish (an extra 0.2 credit cost).<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Internet Orders <C> Internet orders (www.softsim.co.uk) are available for all games here except Advanced Gameplan & Run Chase.<L.31.1>
If you can, please use the website for sending orders - better for me, better for you as it's much quicker and more reliable. You<L.31.1>
need a username to use it, so email and ask for one (don't put a note on your turnsheet, you need to email and ask). You can also<L.31.1>
make credit card payments via softsim.co.uk, although these are generally more expensive than shoving a cheque in the post.....<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Email Both Ways <C> You can use email for your orders, or reports, or both, or neither. They work separately.      <L.31.1>
